    <h1 class="title-article" id="articleContentId">
     基于微信小程序开发的宠物领养平台——代码解读
    </h1>
   </div>
  </div>
 </div>
 <article class="baidu_pl">
  <div class="article_content clearfix" id="article_content">
   <link href="../../assets/css/kdoc_html_views-1a98987dfd.css" rel="stylesheet"/>
   <link href="../../assets/css/ck_htmledit_views-704d5b9767.css" rel="stylesheet"/>
   <div class="markdown_views prism-atom-one-dark" id="content_views">
    <svg style="display: none;" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
     <path d="M5,0 0,2.5 5,5z" id="raphael-marker-block" stroke-linecap="round" style="-webkit-tap-highlight-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0);">
     </path>
    </svg>
    <h2>
     <a id="_0">
     </a>
     项目前端
    </h2>
    <h3>
     <a id="_2">
     </a>
     一、项目的技术架构概况
    </h3>
    <p>
     <strong>
      一句话概括
     </strong>
     ：该项目是基于微信小程序开发的宠物领养平台，采用原生小程序框架进行用户界面的构建，使用
     <code>
      wx.request
     </code>
     进行 API 请求，并通过
     <code>
      getApp()
     </code>
     和本地存储来管理全局状态和用户信息。
    </p>
    <h4>
     <a id="_6">
     </a>
     一）技术栈主要包括
    </h4>
    <ul>
     <li>
      <strong>
       微信小程序框架
      </strong>
      ：项目的核心框架，用于构建用户界面和实现交互逻辑。
     </li>
     <li>
      <strong>
       JavaScript
      </strong>
      ：主要编程语言，项目中的所有逻辑均使用 JavaScript 实现。
     </li>
     <li>
      <strong>
       JSON
      </strong>
      ：用于配置页面和组件的元信息，如页面路径、组件属性等。
     </li>
     <li>
      <strong>
       WXML
      </strong>
      ：类似 HTML 的模板语言，用于定义页面结构。
     </li>
     <li>
      <strong>
       WXSS
      </strong>
      ：类似 CSS 的样式表语言，用于定义页面和组件的样式。
     </li>
     <li>
      <strong>
       本地存储
      </strong>
      ：通过
      <code>
       wx.setStorageSync
      </code>
      和
      <code>
       wx.getStorageSync
      </code>
      管理用户信息和 Token。
     </li>
     <li>
      <strong>
       网络请求
      </strong>
      ：使用
      <code>
       wx.request
      </code>
      进行 API 请求，与后端进行数据交互。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <h4>
     <a id="_16">
     </a>
     二）开发环境要求
    </h4>
    <ul>
     <li>
      <strong>
       微信开发者工具
      </strong>
      ：用于开发和调试微信小程序。
     </li>
     <li>
      <strong>
       IDE
      </strong>
      ：推荐使用 IDEA 或 VS Code，配合微信开发者工具进行开发。
     </li>
     <li>
      <strong>
       依赖管理
      </strong>
      ：通过微信开发者工具自带的依赖管理功能安装和管理项目依赖。
     </li>
     <li>
      <strong>
       浏览器
      </strong>
      ：Edge 或 Chrome，主要用于调试和查看控制台输出。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <h4>
     <a id="_23">
     </a>
     三）项目结构分析
    </h4>
    <pre><code>└── pet_adoption
    ├── backend
    │   ├── src
    │   │   └── main
    │   │       ├── java
    │   │       ├── resources
    │   │       └── webapp
    │   ├── adopt.sql
    │   └── pom.xml
    └── mp-weixin
        ├── components
        │   └── comment
        ├── pages
        │   ├── adopt
        │   ├── blog
        │   ├── comment
        │   ├── index
        │   ├── message
        │   ├── pet
        │   └── user
        ├── static
        │   └── images
        ├── subpackages
        │   ├── comment
        │   └── guide
        ├── utils
        │   └── imagePathUtils.js
        ├── app.js
        ├── app.json
        ├── config.js
        ├── project.config.json
        └── project.private.config.json
</code></pre>
    <h5>
     <a id="_60">
     </a>
     关键目录说明
    </h5>
    <ul>
     <li>
      <strong>
       mp-weixin/
      </strong>
      ：微信小程序的主要目录，包含所有前端代码。
      <ul>
       <li>
        <strong>
         components/
        </strong>
        ：存放可复用的组件，如评论组件。
       </li>
       <li>
        <strong>
         pages/
        </strong>
        ：存放各个页面的代码，每个页面有对应的
        <code>
         .js
        </code>
        、
        <code>
         .json
        </code>
        、
        <code>
         .wxml
        </code>
        和
        <code>
         .wxss
        </code>
        文件。
       </li>
       <li>
        <strong>
         static/
        </strong>
        ：存放静态资源，如图片。
       </li>
       <li>
        <strong>
         subpackages/
        </strong>
        ：存放子包，用于分包加载优化性能。
       </li>
       <li>
        <strong>
         utils/
        </strong>
        ：存放工具函数，如图片路径处理工具。
       </li>
       <li>
        <strong>
         app.js
        </strong>
        ：应用的入口文件，包含全局状态管理和生命周期方法。
       </li>
       <li>
        <strong>
         app.json
        </strong>
        ：应用的全局配置文件，定义了页面路径和窗口表现。
       </li>
       <li>
        <strong>
         config.js
        </strong>
        ：配置文件，定义了不同环境下的 API 地址。
       </li>
      </ul>
     </li>
    </ul>
    <h4>
     <a id="UI_72">
     </a>
     四）UI组件设计
    </h4>
    <h5>
     <a id="1__74">
     </a>
     1. 布局组件
    </h5>
    <ul>
     <li>
      <strong>
       TabBar
      </strong>
      ：项目中使用了 TabBar 进行页面导航，定义在
      <code>
       app.json
      </code>
      中，包含首页、宠物列表和个人中心三个主要页面。
     </li>
     <li>
      <strong>
       Swiper
      </strong>
      ：用于实现轮播图组件，如首页的轮播图展示。
     </li>
     <li>
      <strong>
       Navigator
      </strong>
      ：用于页面之间的跳转，常见于各个页面的跳转按钮。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <h5>
     <a id="2__80">
     </a>
     2. 业务组件
    </h5>
    <ul>
     <li>
      <strong>
       Form 组件
      </strong>
      ：如
      <code>
       adopt/apply.js
      </code>
      中的领养申请表单，实现了表单验证和数据提交功能。
     </li>
     <li>
      <strong>
       List 组件
      </strong>
      ：如
      <code>
       adopt/list.js
      </code>
      中的领养申请列表，支持分页加载、筛选和刷新功能。
     </li>
     <li>
      <strong>
       Modal 组件
      </strong>
      ：用于显示确认对话框，如领养申请的审核通过和拒绝操作。
     </li>
     <li>
      <strong>
       Image 组件
      </strong>
      ：处理图片路径和预览功能，如
      <code>
       blog/publish.js
      </code>
      中的图片上传和预览。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <h5>
     <a id="3__87">
     </a>
     3. 数据流转
    </h5>
    <ul>
     <li>
      <strong>
       Props 和 Events
      </strong>
      ：小程序中通过
      <code>
       data
      </code>
      属性传递数据，通过
      <code>
       bind
      </code>
      方法绑定事件，实现父子组件之间的通信。
     </li>
     <li>
      <strong>
       全局状态管理
      </strong>
      ：通过
      <code>
       getApp()
      </code>
      获取全局应用实例，使用
      <code>
       globalData
      </code>
      管理全局状态，如用户信息、Token 和未读消息数。
     </li>
     <li>
      <strong>
       本地存储
      </strong>
      ：使用
      <code>
       wx.setStorageSync
      </code>
      和
      <code>
       wx.getStorageSync
      </code>
      存储和读取用户信息和 Token，确保用户登录状态的持久化。
     </li>
     <li>
      <strong>
       API 请求
      </strong>
      ：通过
      <code>
       wx.request
      </code>
      发起网络请求，与后端进行数据交互，请求结果通过
      <code>
       Promise
      </code>
      进行处理，确保异步操作的可控性。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <h4>
     <a id="_94">
     </a>
     五）交互实现
    </h4>
    <h5>
     <a id="1__96">
     </a>
     1. 登录与鉴权
    </h5>
    <ul>
     <li>
      <strong>
       登录页面 (
       <code>
        user/login.js
       </code>
       )
      </strong>
      ：提供了微信登录和账号密码登录两种方式，登录成功后保存用户信息和 Token 到本地存储和全局状态中。
     </li>
     <li>
      <strong>
       鉴权拦截
      </strong>
      ：多个页面在
      <code>
       onLoad
      </code>
      或
      <code>
       onShow
      </code>
      生命周期方法中检查用户是否已登录，若未登录则提示用户登录。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <h5>
     <a id="2__101">
     </a>
     2. 数据加载与刷新
    </h5>
    <ul>
     <li>
      <strong>
       下拉刷新
      </strong>
      ：多个页面实现了下拉刷新功能，如
      <code>
       adopt/list.js
      </code>
      和
      <code>
       user/favorite.js
      </code>
      ，通过
      <code>
       onPullDownRefresh
      </code>
      方法触发数据重新加载。
     </li>
     <li>
      <strong>
       上拉加载更多
      </strong>
      ：如
      <code>
       adopt/list.js
      </code>
      和
      <code>
       user/favorite.js
      </code>
      中的
      <code>
       onReachBottom
      </code>
      方法，用于分页加载更多数据。
     </li>
     <li>
      <strong>
       轮询机制
      </strong>
      ：如
      <code>
       message/chat.js
      </code>
      中的
      <code>
       startPolling
      </code>
      方法，通过定时器定期检查新消息。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <h5>
     <a id="3__107">
     </a>
     3. 图片处理
    </h5>
    <ul>
     <li>
      <strong>
       图片上传
      </strong>
      ：如
      <code>
       blog/publish.js
      </code>
      和
      <code>
       blog/edit.js
      </code>
      中的
      <code>
       uploadImages
      </code>
      方法，实现了图片的上传和路径处理。
     </li>
     <li>
      <strong>
       图片预览
      </strong>
      ：多个页面实现了图片预览功能，如
      <code>
       blog/publish.js
      </code>
      中的
      <code>
       previewImage
      </code>
      方法。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <h5>
     <a id="4__112">
     </a>
     4. 表单验证
    </h5>
    <ul>
     <li>
      <strong>
       表单验证
      </strong>
      ：如
      <code>
       adopt/apply.js
      </code>
      中的
      <code>
       validateForm
      </code>
      方法，对表单数据进行验证，确保提交数据的有效性。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <h5>
     <a id="5__116">
     </a>
     5. 路由管理
    </h5>
    <ul>
     <li>
      <strong>
       页面跳转
      </strong>
      ：使用
      <code>
       wx.navigateTo
      </code>
      和
      <code>
       wx.switchTab
      </code>
      实现页面间的跳转，如
      <code>
       index/index.js
      </code>
      中的
      <code>
       navigateToPetDetail
      </code>
      和
      <code>
       navigateToBlogs
      </code>
      方法。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <hr/>
    <p>
     以上是对项目前端部分的详细分析，涵盖了技术架构、组件设计和交互逻辑等方面的内容。该项目采用了原生微信小程序框架，结合了多种交互方式和状态管理手段，确保了良好的用户体验和高效的开发流程。
    </p>
    <h3>
     <a id="___124">
     </a>
     二、主要业务功能在代码中的具体实现 &amp; 调用过程
    </h3>
    <blockquote>
     <p>
      有以下核心业务功能：
     </p>
    </blockquote>
    <ol>
     <li>
      <strong>
       用户认证与权限管理
      </strong>
      - 处理用户登录、权限验证和身份管理。
     </li>
     <li>
      <strong>
       宠物领养管理
      </strong>
      - 包括领养申请、申请详情、申请管理等。
     </li>
     <li>
      <strong>
       宠物信息管理
      </strong>
      - 允许用户查看、发布、编辑和删除宠物信息。
     </li>
     <li>
      <strong>
       故事管理
      </strong>
      - 包括发布故事、编辑故事等。
     </li>
     <li>
      <strong>
       消息管理
      </strong>
      - 用户之间的消息交互。
     </li>
     <li>
      <strong>
       收藏管理
      </strong>
      - 用户可以收藏宠物和博客。
     </li>
     <li>
      <strong>
       用户信息管理
      </strong>
      - 用户可以查看和编辑个人信息。
     </li>
    </ol>
    <h4>
     <a id="1__136">
     </a>
     1. 用户认证与权限管理
    </h4>
    <p>
     <strong>
      设计思路
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      用户通过登录页面提交认证信息。
     </li>
     <li>
      系统后端验证用户信息，并根据用户角色（普通用户、管理员）提供相应权限。
     </li>
     <li>
      用户可以通过微信登录或账号密码登录。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      代码实现逻辑
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      用户填写用户名和密码，选择用户类型后提交表单。
     </li>
     <li>
      后端接收请求，校验用户名和密码的正确性。
     </li>
     <li>
      登录成功后，将用户信息和token存储到本地，并更新全局数据。
     </li>
     <li>
      微信登录通过获取code，发送到后端验证，登录成功后同样存储用户信息和token。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      调用过程
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      用户填写登录信息 -&gt; 提交表单 -&gt; 调用后端登录接口 -&gt; 验证用户信息 -&gt; 返回登录结果 -&gt; 存储用户信息和token -&gt; 更新全局数据。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      代码片段
     </strong>
     (
     <code>
      user/login.js
     </code>
     中的登录部分)：
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-javascript"><span class="token keyword">async</span> <span class="token function">onLogin</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
  <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>data<span class="token punctuation">.</span>loading<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token keyword">return</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
  <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token operator">!</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>data<span class="token punctuation">.</span>isAgree<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setData</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token literal-property property">errorMsg</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">'请先同意用户协议和隐私政策'</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">return</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
  <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
  <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token operator">!</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>data<span class="token punctuation">.</span>username <span class="token operator">||</span> <span class="token operator">!</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>data<span class="token punctuation">.</span>password<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setData</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token literal-property property">errorMsg</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">'请输入用户名和密码'</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">return</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
  <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
  <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setData</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token literal-property property">loading</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">errorMsg</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">''</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
  <span class="token keyword">try</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">const</span> res <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">await</span> wx<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">request</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>

      <span class="token keyword">const</span> userData <span class="token operator">=</span> res<span class="token punctuation">.</span>data<span class="token punctuation">.</span>data<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
      wx<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setStorageSync</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'userInfo'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> userData<span class="token punctuation">.</span>user<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

      wx<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setStorageSync</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'userId'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> userData<span class="token punctuation">.</span>user<span class="token punctuation">.</span>id<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
      app<span class="token punctuation">.</span>globalData<span class="token punctuation">.</span>userInfo <span class="token operator">=</span> userData<span class="token punctuation">.</span>user<span class="token punctuation">;</span>

    <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setData</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token literal-property property">loading</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">false</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
  <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</code></pre>
    <h4>
     <a id="2__204">
     </a>
     2. 宠物领养管理
    </h4>
    <p>
     <strong>
      设计思路
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      用户可以申请领养宠物，填写相关信息。
     </li>
     <li>
      管理员或宠物发布者可以审核领养申请。
     </li>
     <li>
      用户可以查看领养申请的详细信息。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      代码实现逻辑
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      用户填写领养申请表单，提交后发送至后端。
     </li>
     <li>
      后端验证表单信息，并存储申请记录。
     </li>
     <li>
      管理员或宠物发布者可以在列表中查看申请，进行审核操作。
     </li>
     <li>
      审核通过或拒绝后，更新申请状态，并通知相关用户。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      调用过程
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      用户填写领养申请表单 -&gt; 提交表单 -&gt; 调用后端接口 -&gt; 存储申请记录 -&gt; 管理员或宠物发布者查看申请 -&gt; 审核通过或拒绝 -&gt; 更新申请状态。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      代码片段
     </strong>
     (
     <code>
      adopt/apply.js
     </code>
     中的表单提交部分)：
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-javascript"><span class="token function">submitForm</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">e</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
  <span class="token keyword">const</span> formData <span class="token operator">=</span> e<span class="token punctuation">.</span>detail<span class="token punctuation">.</span>value<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
  <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token operator">!</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">validateForm</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>formData<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token keyword">return</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
  <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setData</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token literal-property property">submitting</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
  <span class="token keyword">const</span> requestData <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token literal-property property">petId</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>data<span class="token punctuation">.</span>petId<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token literal-property property">remark</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token constant">JSON</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">stringify</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
      <span class="token literal-property property">name</span><span class="token operator">:</span> formData<span class="token punctuation">.</span>name<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
      <span class="token literal-property property">phone</span><span class="token operator">:</span> formData<span class="token punctuation">.</span>phone<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
      <span class="token literal-property property">wechat</span><span class="token operator">:</span> formData<span class="token punctuation">.</span>wechat<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
      <span class="token literal-property property">address</span><span class="token operator">:</span> formData<span class="token punctuation">.</span>address<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
      <span class="token literal-property property">houseType</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>data<span class="token punctuation">.</span>houseTypes<span class="token punctuation">[</span>formData<span class="token punctuation">.</span>houseTypeIndex<span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
      <span class="token literal-property property">isRent</span><span class="token operator">:</span> formData<span class="token punctuation">.</span>isRent<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
      <span class="token literal-property property">landlordAgree</span><span class="token operator">:</span> formData<span class="token punctuation">.</span>landlordAgree<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
      <span class="token literal-property property">familyMembers</span><span class="token operator">:</span> formData<span class="token punctuation">.</span>familyMembers<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
      <span class="token literal-property property">familyAgree</span><span class="token operator">:</span> formData<span class="token punctuation">.</span>familyAgree<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
      <span class="token literal-property property">hasPetExperience</span><span class="token operator">:</span> formData<span class="token punctuation">.</span>hasPetExperience<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
      <span class="token literal-property property">description</span><span class="token operator">:</span> formData<span class="token punctuation">.</span>description
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
  wx<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">request</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token literal-property property">url</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token template-string"><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">${<!-- --></span>app<span class="token punctuation">.</span>globalData<span class="token punctuation">.</span>baseUrl<span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token string">/adopt/apply</span><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span></span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token literal-property property">method</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">'POST'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token literal-property property">header</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
      <span class="token string-property property">'Content-Type'</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">'application/json'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
      <span class="token string-property property">'Authorization'</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token template-string"><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span><span class="token string">Bearer </span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">${<!-- --></span>wx<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getStorageSync</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'token'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span></span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token literal-property property">data</span><span class="token operator">:</span> requestData<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token function-variable function">success</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">res</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
      <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>res<span class="token punctuation">.</span>data<span class="token punctuation">.</span>code <span class="token operator">===</span> <span class="token number">200</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
        wx<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">showToast</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token literal-property property">title</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">'申请提交成功'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">icon</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">'success'</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

          <span class="token keyword">const</span> prevPage <span class="token operator">=</span> pages<span class="token punctuation">[</span>pages<span class="token punctuation">.</span>length <span class="token operator">-</span> <span class="token number">2</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

    <h4>
     <a id="3__276">
     </a>
     3. 宠物信息管理
    </h4>
    <p>
     <strong>
      设计思路
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      用户可以查看宠物列表、发布新宠物、编辑已有的宠物信息。
     </li>
     <li>
      宠物信息包括图片、描述等。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      代码实现逻辑
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      前端展示宠物列表，用户可以选择查看、发布或编辑宠物。
     </li>
     <li>
      发布和编辑宠物时，用户可以上传图片并填写相关信息。
     </li>
     <li>
      提交后，后端验证并存储宠物信息。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      调用过程
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      用户查看宠物列表 -&gt; 点击发布或编辑 -&gt; 填写宠物信息 -&gt; 提交表单 -&gt; 调用后端接口 -&gt; 存储宠物信息。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      代码片段
     </strong>
     (
     <code>
      pet/publish.js
     </code>
     中的宠物发布部分)：
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-javascript"><span class="token keyword">async</span> <span class="token function">submitForm</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">e</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
  <span class="token keyword">try</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">const</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> title<span class="token punctuation">,</span> content <span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>data<span class="token punctuation">.</span>formData<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token operator">!</span>title<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">trim</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
      wx<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">showToast</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token literal-property property">title</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">'请输入故事标题'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">icon</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">'none'</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
      <span class="token keyword">return</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token operator">!</span>content<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">trim</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>

    <h4>
     <a id="4__346">
     </a>
     4. 故事管理
    </h4>
    <p>
     <strong>
      设计思路
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      用户可以发布新的故事，编辑已有的故事。
     </li>
     <li>
      故事包括标题、内容、封面图片和标签。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      代码实现逻辑
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      用户填写故事标题、内容、选择封面图片和标签。
     </li>
     <li>
      提交后，后端验证并存储故事信息。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      调用过程
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      用户填写故事信息 -&gt; 提交表单 -&gt; 调用后端接口 -&gt; 存储故事信息。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      代码片段
     </strong>
     (
     <code>
      blog/publish.js
     </code>
     中的故事发布部分)：
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-javascript"><span class="token function">submitForm</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">e</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
  <span class="token keyword">try</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">const</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> title<span class="token punctuation">,</span> content <span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>data<span class="token punctuation">.</span>formData<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token operator">!</span>title<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">trim</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
      wx<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">showToast</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token literal-property property">title</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">'请输入故事标题'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">icon</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">'none'</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
      <span class="token keyword">return</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token operator">!</span>content<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">trim</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
      wx<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">showToast</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token literal-property property">title</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">'请输入故事内容'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">icon</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">'none'</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
      <span class="token keyword">return</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>

      wx<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">showToast</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token literal-property property">title</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">'请至少上传一张图片'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">icon</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">'none'</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
      <span class="token keyword">return</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    wx<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">showLoading</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token literal-property property">title</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">'正在发布...'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">mask</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

    <h4>
     <a id="5__422">
     </a>
     5. 消息管理
    </h4>
    <p>
     <strong>
      设计思路
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      用户之间可以进行消息交流。
     </li>
     <li>
      消息包括文本、图片等内容。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      代码实现逻辑
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      用户发送消息，消息存储到数据库。
     </li>
     <li>
      消息列表页面展示用户之间的消息，并支持加载更多。
     </li>
     <li>
      消息实时轮询，保证用户及时看到新消息。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      调用过程
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      用户输入消息内容 -&gt; 点击发送 -&gt; 调用后端接口 -&gt; 存储消息 -&gt; 更新消息列表 -&gt; 实时轮询新消息。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      代码片段
     </strong>
     (
     <code>
      message/chat.js
     </code>
     中的消息发送部分)：
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-javascript"><span class="token keyword">async</span> <span class="token function">sendMessage</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>

    <h4>
     <a id="6__475">
     </a>
     6. 收藏管理
    </h4>
    <p>
     <strong>
      设计思路
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      用户可以收藏感兴趣的宠物和博客。
     </li>
     <li>
      用户可以查看已收藏的宠物和博客，并进行取消收藏操作。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      代码实现逻辑
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      用户点击收藏按钮，后端记录收藏信息。
     </li>
     <li>
      用户可以在收藏页面查看已收藏的内容，并进行取消收藏操作。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      调用过程
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      用户点击收藏按钮 -&gt; 调用后端接口 -&gt; 记录收藏信息 -&gt; 用户查看收藏列表 -&gt; 取消收藏 -&gt; 调用取消收藏接口。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      代码片段
     </strong>
     (
     <code>
      user/favorite.js
     </code>
     中的收藏部分)：
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-javascript"><span class="token keyword">async</span> <span class="token function">onFavoriteTap</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">e</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>

  <span class="token keyword">try</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>

    <h4>
     <a id="7__522">
     </a>
     7. 用户信息管理
    </h4>
    <p>
     <strong>
      设计思路
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      用户可以查看和编辑个人信息。
     </li>
     <li>
      用户可以上传头像、修改昵称、真实姓名、电话号码等。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      代码实现逻辑
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      用户选择头像或填写个人信息。
     </li>
     <li>
      提交后，后端验证并更新用户信息。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      调用过程
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      用户选择头像或填写信息 -&gt; 提交表单 -&gt; 调用后端接口 -&gt; 更新用户信息。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      代码片段
     </strong>
     (
     <code>
      user/profile.js
     </code>
     中的用户信息保存部分)：
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-javascript"><span class="token keyword">async</span> <span class="token function">onSave</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
  <span class="token keyword">try</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>data<span class="token punctuation">.</span>userInfo<span class="token punctuation">.</span>telephone <span class="token operator">&amp;&amp;</span> <span class="token operator">!</span><span class="token regex"><span class="token regex-delimiter">/</span><span class="token regex-source language-regex">^1[3-9]\d{9}$</span><span class="token regex-delimiter">/</span></span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">test</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>data<span class="token punctuation">.</span>userInfo<span class="token punctuation">.</span>telephone<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
      wx<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">showToast</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token literal-property property">title</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">'手机号码格式不正确'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">icon</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">'none'</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
      <span class="token keyword">return</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>data<span class="token punctuation">.</span>userInfo<span class="token punctuation">.</span>email <span class="token operator">&amp;&amp;</span> <span class="token operator">!</span><span class="token regex"><span class="token regex-delimiter">/</span><span class="token regex-source language-regex">^[a-zA-Z0-9_-]+@[a-zA-Z0-9_-]+(\.[a-zA-Z0-9_-]+)+$</span><span class="token regex-delimiter">/</span></span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">test</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>data<span class="token punctuation">.</span>userInfo<span class="token punctuation">.</span>email<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
      wx<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">showToast</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token literal-property property">title</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">'邮箱格式不正确'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">icon</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">'none'</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
      <span class="token keyword">return</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    wx<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">showLoading</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token literal-property property">title</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">'保存中...'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">mask</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">const</span> updateData <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
      <span class="token literal-property property">id</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>data<span class="token punctuation">.</span>userInfo<span class="token punctuation">.</span>id<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
      <span class="token operator">...</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>data<span class="token punctuation">.</span>userInfo
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">const</span> res <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">await</span> wx<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">request</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>

    <h4>
     <a id="8__583">
     </a>
     8. 首页展示与导航
    </h4>
    <p>
     <strong>
      设计思路
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      首页展示轮播图、推荐宠物和最新故事，吸引用户关注。
     </li>
     <li>
      提供导航功能，用户可以跳转到不同的页面。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      代码实现逻辑
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      加载轮播图、推荐宠物和最新故事的数据。
     </li>
     <li>
      处理图片路径，确保显示正确的图片。
     </li>
     <li>
      提供跳转功能，如跳转到宠物详情、博客详情、发布宠物等。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      调用过程
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      页面加载 -&gt; 初始化数据 -&gt; 加载轮播图、推荐宠物和最新故事 -&gt; 展示数据 -&gt; 用户点击跳转 -&gt; 导航到对应页面。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      代码片段
     </strong>
     (
     <code>
      index/index.js
     </code>
     中的首页加载部分)：
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-javascript"><span class="token function-variable function">initData</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>

    <h4>
     <a id="9__633">
     </a>
     9. 忘记密码
    </h4>
    <p>
     <strong>
      设计思路
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      用户可以通过手机号找回密码。
     </li>
     <li>
      系统验证用户信息并重置密码。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      代码实现逻辑
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      用户输入用户名、手机号和新密码。
     </li>
     <li>
      系统验证手机号格式和密码一致性。
     </li>
     <li>
      发送重置密码请求到后端。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      调用过程
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      用户输入信息 -&gt; 提交表单 -&gt; 验证信息 -&gt; 调用后端接口 -&gt; 重置密码 -&gt; 返回结果。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      代码片段
     </strong>
     (
     <code>
      user/forgot-password.js
     </code>
     中的重置密码部分)：
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-javascript"><span class="token keyword">async</span> <span class="token function">onResetPassword</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>

  <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token operator">!</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>data<span class="token punctuation">.</span>userName <span class="token operator">||</span> <span class="token operator">!</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>data<span class="token punctuation">.</span>telephone<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setData</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token literal-property property">errorMsg</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">'请输入用户名和手机号'</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

  <span class="token punctuation">}</span>

        wx<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">navigateBack</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
      <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token number">1500</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token keyword">else</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
      <span class="token keyword">throw</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">Error</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>res<span class="token punctuation">.</span>data<span class="token punctuation">.</span>message <span class="token operator">||</span> <span class="token string">'未知错误'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
  <span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token keyword">catch</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>error<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setData</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token literal-property property">errorMsg</span><span class="token operator">:</span> error<span class="token punctuation">.</span>message <span class="token operator">||</span> <span class="token string">'重置密码失败，请重试'</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
  <span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token keyword">finally</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setData</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token literal-property property">loading</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">false</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
  <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</code></pre>
    <h4>
     <a id="10__699">
     </a>
     10. 用户设置
    </h4>
    <p>
     <strong>
      设计思路
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      用户可以修改通知设置、切换深色模式、修改密码、清除缓存和退出登录。
     </li>
     <li>
      提供关于我们的页面链接。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      代码实现逻辑
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      用户选择设置项，如修改通知设置、切换深色模式等。
     </li>
     <li>
      修改密码时，用户输入旧密码和新密码，后端验证并更新密码。
     </li>
     <li>
      清除缓存时，删除本地存储的所有数据。
     </li>
     <li>
      退出登录时，清除用户信息并返回登录页。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      调用过程
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      用户选择设置项 -&gt; 修改设置 -&gt; 更新本地存储或调用后端接口 -&gt; 返回结果。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      代码片段
     </strong>
     (
     <code>
      user/settings.js
     </code>
     中的修改密码部分)：
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-javascript"><span class="token function-variable function">changePassword</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>

            <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>res<span class="token punctuation">.</span>data<span class="token punctuation">.</span>code <span class="token operator">===</span> <span class="token number">0</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>

                wx<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">reLaunch</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token literal-property property">url</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">'/pages/user/index'</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

    <h4>
     <a id="11__760">
     </a>
     11. 宠物详情与编辑
    </h4>
    <p>
     <strong>
      设计思路
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      用户可以查看宠物的详细信息，包括图片、描述等。
     </li>
     <li>
      用户可以编辑已发布的宠物信息。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      代码实现逻辑
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      加载宠物详情数据，处理图片路径。
     </li>
     <li>
      编辑宠物时，用户可以修改图片、描述等信息。
     </li>
     <li>
      提交编辑内容，后端验证并更新宠物信息。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      调用过程
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      用户查看宠物详情 -&gt; 加载数据 -&gt; 用户点击编辑 -&gt; 修改信息 -&gt; 提交表单 -&gt; 更新宠物信息。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      代码片段
     </strong>
     (
     <code>
      pet/detail.js
     </code>
     中的宠物详情加载部分)：
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-javascript"><span class="token function">loadPetDetail</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>

    <span class="token literal-property property">url</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token template-string"><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">${<!-- --></span>app<span class="token punctuation">.</span>globalData<span class="token punctuation">.</span>baseUrl<span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token string">/pets/</span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">${<!-- --></span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>data<span class="token punctuation">.</span>petId<span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span></span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
    <span class="token function-variable function">success</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">res</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
      <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>res<span class="token punctuation">.</span>statusCode <span class="token operator">===</span> <span class="token number">200</span> <span class="token operator">&amp;&amp;</span> res<span class="token punctuation">.</span>data<span class="token punctuation">.</span>code <span class="token operator">===</span> <span class="token number">200</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>

            <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token operator">!</span>pic<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">startsWith</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'http'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token operator">&amp;&amp;</span> <span class="token operator">!</span>pic<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">startsWith</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'https'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>

</code></pre>
    <h4>
     <a id="12__814">
     </a>
     12. 领养申请管理
    </h4>
    <p>
     <strong>
      设计思路
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      用户可以查看和管理领养申请，包括通过和拒绝申请。
     </li>
     <li>
      管理员可以查看所有领养申请，并进行批量审核。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      代码实现逻辑
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      加载领养申请列表，处理图片路径。
     </li>
     <li>
      管理员或宠物发布者可以审核申请，填写拒绝理由。
     </li>
     <li>
      审核通过或拒绝后，更新申请状态，并通知相关用户。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      调用过程
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      用户查看领养申请列表 -&gt; 加载数据 -&gt; 用户点击审核 -&gt; 填写拒绝理由 -&gt; 提交审核 -&gt; 更新申请状态。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      代码片段
     </strong>
     (
     <code>
      adopt/manage.js
     </code>
     中的领养申请审核部分)：
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-javascript"><span class="token keyword">async</span> <span class="token function">updateAdoptStatus</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">e</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
  <span class="token keyword">const</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> id<span class="token punctuation">,</span> status <span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> e<span class="token punctuation">.</span>currentTarget<span class="token punctuation">.</span>dataset<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
  <span class="token keyword">try</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">const</span> res <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">await</span> wx<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">request</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
      <span class="token literal-property property">url</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token template-string"><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">${<!-- --></span>app<span class="token punctuation">.</span>globalData<span class="token punctuation">.</span>baseUrl<span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token string">/adopt/status</span><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span></span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
      <span class="token literal-property property">method</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">'PUT'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
      <span class="token literal-property property">data</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> id<span class="token punctuation">,</span> status <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
      <span class="token literal-property property">header</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token string-property property">'Authorization'</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token template-string"><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span><span class="token string">Bearer </span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">${<!-- --></span>wx<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getStorageSync</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'token'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span></span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string-property property">'Content-Type'</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">'application/json'</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>res<span class="token punctuation">.</span>data<span class="token punctuation">.</span>code <span class="token operator">===</span> <span class="token number">200</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
      wx<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">showToast</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token literal-property property">title</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">'更新成功'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">icon</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">'success'</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
      <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">loadAdoptions</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token keyword">else</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
      <span class="token keyword">throw</span> <span class="token keyword">new</span> <span class="token class-name">Error</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>res<span class="token punctuation">.</span>data<span class="token punctuation">.</span>message <span class="token operator">||</span> <span class="token string">'更新失败'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
  <span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token keyword">catch</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>error<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    wx<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">showToast</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token literal-property property">title</span><span class="token operator">:</span> error<span class="token punctuation">.</span>message <span class="token operator">||</span> <span class="token string">'更新失败'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">icon</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">'none'</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
  <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</code></pre>
    <h4>
     <a id="13__855">
     </a>
     13. 用户收藏管理
    </h4>
    <p>
     <strong>
      设计思路
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      用户可以收藏宠物和博客。
     </li>
     <li>
      用户可以在收藏页面查看和取消收藏。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      代码实现逻辑
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      加载用户收藏的宠物和博客列表。
     </li>
     <li>
      用户点击取消收藏按钮，发送请求到后端。
     </li>
     <li>
      成功取消收藏后，更新本地收藏列表。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      调用过程
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      用户进入收藏页面 -&gt; 加载收藏列表 -&gt; 用户点击取消收藏 -&gt; 发送请求 -&gt; 更新收藏列表。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      代码片段
     </strong>
     (
     <code>
      user/favorite.js
     </code>
     中的取消收藏部分)：
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-javascript"><span class="token keyword">async</span> <span class="token function">onFavoriteTap</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">e</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>

  <span class="token keyword">const</span> token <span class="token operator">=</span> wx<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">getStorageSync</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">'token'</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
  <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token operator">!</span>token<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token keyword">return</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
  <span class="token keyword">try</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">const</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> type <span class="token operator">===</span> <span class="token string">'pet'</span> <span class="token operator">?</span> <span class="token template-string"><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">${<!-- --></span>app<span class="token punctuation">.</span>globalData<span class="token punctuation">.</span>baseUrl<span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token string">/favorites/remove/</span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">${<!-- --></span>id<span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span></span> <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token template-string"><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">${<!-- --></span>app<span class="token punctuation">.</span>globalData<span class="token punctuation">.</span>baseUrl<span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token string">/blog/favorites/remove</span><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span></span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">const</span> data <span class="token operator">=</span> type <span class="token operator">===</span> <span class="token string">'pet'</span> <span class="token operator">?</span> <span class="token keyword">null</span> <span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token literal-property property">blogId</span><span class="token operator">:</span> id <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

    <span class="token keyword">const</span> res <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">await</span> wx<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">request</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
      url<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
      method<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
      <span class="token literal-property property">header</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token string-property property">'Authorization'</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token template-string"><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span><span class="token string">Bearer </span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">${<!-- --></span>token<span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span></span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string-property property">'Content-Type'</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">'application/json'</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
      data
    <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
    <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>res<span class="token punctuation">.</span>data<span class="token punctuation">.</span>code <span class="token operator">===</span> <span class="token number">200</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>

      <span class="token keyword">const</span> list <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>data<span class="token punctuation">[</span>listKey<span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">filter</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">item</span> <span class="token operator">=&gt;</span> item<span class="token punctuation">.</span>id <span class="token operator">!==</span> id<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
      <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">setData</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span>listKey<span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token operator">:</span> list <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
      wx<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">showToast</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span> <span class="token literal-property property">title</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">'已取消收藏'</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token literal-property property">icon</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">'success'</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>

  <span class="token punctuation">}</span> <span class="token keyword">catch</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>error<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>

  <span class="token punctuation">}</span>
<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</code></pre>
    <h4>
     <a id="14__903">
     </a>
     14. 用户注册
    </h4>
    <p>
     <strong>
      设计思路
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      新用户可以通过填写注册信息来创建账户。
     </li>
     <li>
      注册信息包括用户名、密码、真实姓名、手机号等。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      代码实现逻辑
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      用户填写注册信息，提交表单。
     </li>
     <li>
      后端验证注册信息的合法性，并创建新用户。
     </li>
     <li>
      注册成功后，返回登录页。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      调用过程
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      用户填写注册信息 -&gt; 提交表单 -&gt; 验证信息 -&gt; 调用后端接口 -&gt; 创建新用户 -&gt; 返回登录页。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      代码片段
     </strong>
     (
     <code>
      user/register.js
     </code>
     中的注册部分)：
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-javascript"><span class="token keyword">async</span> <span class="token function">onRegister</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
  <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token operator">!</span><span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">validateForm</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token keyword">return</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
  <span class="token keyword">try</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
    <span class="token keyword">const</span> res <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">await</span> wx<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">request</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
      <span class="token literal-property property">url</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token template-string"><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">${<!-- --></span>app<span class="token punctuation">.</span>globalData<span class="token punctuation">.</span>baseUrl<span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token string">/user/register</span><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span></span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>

<span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</code></pre>
    <h4>
     <a id="15__959">
     </a>
     15. 用户评论管理
    </h4>
    <p>
     <strong>
      设计思路
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      用户可以查看和删除自己的评论。
     </li>
     <li>
      用户可以对宠物或博客发表评论。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      代码实现逻辑
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      加载用户评论列表，处理图片路径。
     </li>
     <li>
      用户点击删除按钮，发送请求到后端。
     </li>
     <li>
      成功删除评论后，更新本地评论列表。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      调用过程
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      用户进入评论页面 -&gt; 加载评论列表 -&gt; 用户点击删除 -&gt; 发送请求 -&gt; 更新评论列表。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      代码片段
     </strong>
     (
     <code>
      user/comments.js
     </code>
     中的删除评论部分)：
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-javascript"><span class="token function-variable function">deleteComment</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token keyword">function</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">e</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>

    <h4>
     <a id="16__1008">
     </a>
     16. 消息轮询与通知
    </h4>
    <p>
     <strong>
      设计思路
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      实现实时消息轮询，确保用户能及时看到新消息。
     </li>
     <li>
      消息轮询定时器每30秒检查一次未读消息。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      代码实现逻辑
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      在应用启动和前台显示时，启动消息轮询定时器。
     </li>
     <li>
      每30秒调用一次未读消息接口，检查是否有新消息。
     </li>
     <li>
      如果有新消息，更新全局未读消息计数，并显示小红点。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      调用过程
     </strong>
     ：
    </p>
    <ul>
     <li>
      应用启动或进入前台 -&gt; 启动消息轮询 -&gt; 定时检查未读消息 -&gt; 更新未读消息计数 -&gt; 显示小红点。
     </li>
    </ul>
    <p>
     <strong>
      代码片段
     </strong>
     (
     <code>
      mp-weixin/app.js
     </code>
     中的消息轮询部分)：
    </p>
    <pre><code class="prism language-javascript"><span class="token function">startCheckingMessages</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>

  <span class="token keyword">this</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span>globalData<span class="token punctuation">.</span>messagePollingTimer <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">setInterval</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token punctuation">{<!-- --></span>
